(_( 6_CD )_) purchasers_NNS and_CC keepers_NNS as_IN to_TO the_DT method_NN of_IN utilizing_VBG the_DT services_NNS of_IN the_DT two_CD classes_NNS of_IN bulls_NNS ,_, viz._NN ,_, of_IN the_DT submontane_NN and_CC western_JJ breeds_NNS which_WDT are_VBP entirely_RB different_JJ in_IN their_PRP$ nature_NN and_CC habits_NNS and_CC each_DT requires_VBZ a_DT different_JJ line_NN of_IN treatment_NN ._.
Class_NN (_( 1_CD )_) viz._NN ,_, those_DT bred_VBN at_IN the_DT Kheri_NNP farm_NN ,_, are_VBP of_IN a_DT semi-wild_JJ disposition_NN ,_, and_CC can_MD not_RB be_VB managed_VBN in_IN the_DT same_JJ way_NN as_IN the_DT more_RBR domesticated_JJ breeds_NNS ._.
